### React AdvancedRadio Currency Example

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/Inputs/advanced-radio

This snippet demonstrates how to use the RizzUI AdvancedRadio component to create a currency selection interface. It displays four currency options (Taka, Dollar, Euro, Pound) with corresponding icons and labels, utilizing React and JSX.

```jsx
import { AdvancedRadio } from "rizzui";
import { CurrencyBangladeshiIcon, CurrencyDollarIcon, CurrencyEuroIcon, CurrencyPoundIcon } from "@/components/icons";
import { Text } from "@/components/ui/text";

export default function App() {
  return (
    <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-4 gap-6">
      <AdvancedRadio
        name="currency"
        value="taka"
        defaultChecked
      >
        <CurrencyBangladeshiIcon className="w-7 h-auto mb-4" />
        <Text className="font-semibold">Taka</Text>
      </AdvancedRadio>
      <AdvancedRadio
        name="currency"
        value="dollar"
      >
        <CurrencyDollarIcon className="w-7 h-auto mb-4" />
        <Text className="font-semibold">Dollar</Text>
      </AdvancedRadio>
      <AdvancedRadio
        name="currency"
        value="euro"
      >
        <CurrencyEuroIcon className="w-7 h-auto mb-4" />
        <Text className="font-semibold">Euro</Text>
      </AdvancedRadio>
      <AdvancedRadio
        name="currency"
        value="pound"
      >
        <CurrencyPoundIcon className="w-7 h-auto mb-4" />
        <Text className="font-semibold">Pound</Text>
      </AdvancedRadio>
    </div>
  );
}
```

--------------------------------

### RizzUI Grid.Col Component API Reference

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/0.8.7/layouts/grid

API documentation for the RizzUI Grid.Col component, detailing props for column and row positioning and spanning, including `as`, `colStart`, `colEnd`, `colSpan`, `order`, `rowStart`, `rowEnd`, `rowSpan`, and `placeSelf`.

```APIDOC
Grid.Col Props:
  as: (string) Render as a specific HTML element (default: 'div').
  colStart: (ColumnStartType) Defines the starting column line for the grid item.
  colEnd: (ColumnEndType) Defines the ending column line for the grid item.
  colSpan: (ColumnSpanType) Defines the size of the grid item by specifying how many columns it should span.
  order: (OrderType) Specifies the order in which a grid item appears in its grid area.
  rowStart: (RowStartType) Defines the starting row line for the grid item.
  rowEnd: (RowEndType) Defines the ending row line for the grid item.
  rowSpan: (RowSpanType) Defines the size of the grid item by specifying how many rows it should span.
  placeSelf: (PlaceSelfType) Defines the position of an item within its grid area, overriding any container-level alignment.
```

### FileInput Component API

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/0.8.7/Inputs/fileinput

API documentation for the RizzUI FileInput component, detailing its available props for customization.

```APIDOC
FileInput:
  Props:
    label: string
      - Description: The label text displayed for the input field.
      - Required: Yes
    variant: "outline" | "flat" | "text"
      - Description: Controls the visual style of the FileInput.
      - Default: "outline"
    size: "sm" | "" | "lg" | "xl"
      - Description: Determines the size of the FileInput component.
      - Default: ""
    // Other common input props like className, disabled, etc. are also supported.
```

### RizzUI FileInput Component API Reference

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/Inputs/fileinput

Comprehensive API documentation for the RizzUI FileInput component, detailing all available props, their types, descriptions, default values, and related type definitions.

```APIDOC
FileInput Props:
  label: ReactNode | Set field label | __
  labelWeight: LabelWeight | Set label font weight | "medium"
  variant: FileinputVariants | The variants of the component are: | "outline"
  size: FileinputSizes | The size of the component. "sm" is equivalent to the dense input styling. | "md"
  rounded: FileinputRounded | The rounded variants are: | "md"
  placeholder: string | Set input placeholder text | __
  disabled: boolean | Whether the input is disabled or not | __
  clearable: boolean | add clearable option | __
  onClear: FileinputOnclear | clear event | __
  helperText: ReactNode | Add helper text. It could be string or a React component | __
  error: string | Show error message using this prop | __
  labelClassName: string | Override default CSS style of label | __
  inputClassName: string | Override default CSS style of input | __
  helperClassName: string | Override default CSS style of helperText | __
  errorClassName: string | Override default CSS style of error message | __
  className: string | Add custom classes to the root of the component | __
  ref: Ref<HTMLInputElement> |  | __
  ...: InputHTMLAttributes | native props like **value**, **onChange**, **onFocus**, **onBlur** ... | __

Fileinput Variants Type:
  type FileinputVariants = "outline" | "flat" | "text";

Label Weight Type:
  type LabelWeight = "normal" | "medium" | "semibold" | "bold";

Fileinput Sizes Type:
  type FileinputSizes = "sm" | "md" | "lg" | "xl";

Fileinput Rounded Type:
  type FileinputRounded = "sm" | "md" | "lg" | "none" | "pill";

Fileinput Onclear Type:
  type FileinputOnclear = () => void;

```

### Simple Accordion Example

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/data-display/accordion

Demonstrates a basic implementation of the RizzUI Accordion component in React. It uses sample data to render multiple collapsible panels, each with a title and content. Dependencies include the 'rizzui' library and '@heroicons/react'.

```jsx
"use client";

import { Accordion } from "rizzui";
import { ChevronDownIcon } from "@heroicons/react/24/solid";

// Assuming 'cn' is a utility function for class merging, e.g., from 'clsx'
// import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"; 

const data = [
  {
    title: "Option A",
    content: `
      If you are unhappy with your purchase for any reason, email us within 90
      days and we will refund you in full, no questions asked. If you are
      unhappy with your purchase for any reason, email us within 90 days and
      we will refund you in full, no questions asked.If you are unhappy with
      your purchase for any reason.
    `,
  },
  // ... potentially more data items
];

export default function App() {
  return (
    <>
    {data.map((item) => (
      <Accordion
        key={item.title}
        className="mx-8 border-b last-of-type:border-b-0"
      >
        <Accordion.Header>
          {({ open }) => (
            <div className="flex w-full cursor-pointer items-center justify-between py-5 text-xl font-semibold">
              {item.title}
              <ChevronDownIcon
                className={cn(
                  "h-5 w-5 -rotate-90 transform transition-transform duration-300",
                  open && "-rotate-0"
                )}
              />
            </div>
          )}
        </Accordion.Header>
        <Accordion.Body className="mb-7">{item.content}</Accordion.Body>
      </Accordion>
    ))}
    </>
  );
}

```

### RizzUI Tooltip Placement Example

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/overlays/tooltip

Demonstrates how to use the RizzUI Tooltip component with various placement options (left, right, top, bottom, etc.) in a React application. It showcases different positioning strategies for the tooltip relative to its trigger element.

```javascript
"use client";

import { Tooltip, Button } from "rizzui";

export default function App() {
  return (
    <div className="flex h-[560px] flex-col">
      <div className="relative m-auto flex h-96 max-w-xl w-full flex-wrap justify-center gap-8">
        <Tooltip content={"Left"} placement="left">
          <Button variant="outline" className="absolute top-1/2 left-0">
            L
          </Button>
        </Tooltip>
        <Tooltip content={"Right"} placement="right">
          <Button variant="outline" className="absolute top-1/2 right-0">
            R
          </Button>
        </Tooltip>
        <Tooltip content={"Top"} placement="top">
          <Button variant="outline" className="absolute top-0">
            T
          </Button>
        </Tooltip>
        <Tooltip content={"Bottom"} placement="bottom">
          <Button variant="outline" className="absolute -bottom-5">
            B
          </Button>
        </Tooltip>
        <Tooltip content={"Top Start"} placement="top-start">
          <Button
            variant="outline"
            className="absolute left-10 xl:left-20 top-0"
          >
            TS
          </Button>
        </Tooltip>
        <Tooltip content={"Top End"} placement="top-end">
          <Button
            variant="outline"
            className="absolute top-0 right-10 xl:right-20"
          >
            TE
          </Button>
        </Tooltip>
        <Tooltip content={"Bottom Start"} placement="bottom-start">
          <Button
            variant="outline"
            className="absolute -bottom-5 left-10 xl:left-20"
          >
            BS
          </Button>
        </Tooltip>
        <Tooltip content={"Bottom End"} placement="bottom-end">
          <Button
            variant="outline"
            className="absolute -bottom-5 right-10 xl:right-20"
          >
            BE
          </Button>
        </Tooltip>
        <Tooltip content={"Left Start"} placement="left-start">
          <Button variant="outline" className="absolute left-8 top-24">
            LS
          </Button>
        </Tooltip>
        <Tooltip content={"Left End"} placement="left-end">
          <Button variant="outline" className="absolute bottom-16 left-8">
            LE
          </Button>
        </Tooltip>
        <Tooltip content={"Right Start"} placement="right-start">
          <Button variant="outline" className="absolute right-8 top-24">
            RS
          </Button>
        </Tooltip>
        <Tooltip content={"Right End"} placement="right-end">
          <Button variant="outline" className="absolute right-8 bottom-16">
            RE
          </Button>
        </Tooltip>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

```

```javascript
        className="flex-wrap"

        on our every product
      </Announcement>
      <Announcement
        className="flex-wrap"
        badgeText="Trending"
        highlightedText="25% discount"
        color="danger"

    </>
```

### ActionIcon: API Reference (APIDOC)

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/buttons/action-icon

Comprehensive API documentation for the RizzUI ActionIcon component, detailing all available props, their types, default values, and descriptions. Includes related type definitions for variants, sizes, and rounded properties.

```APIDOC
ActionIcon Props:
  as: button | span
    Description: Render as the component. Defaults to "button".
    Default: "button"
  children: React.ReactNode
    Description: Use any SVG icon as the content of the ActionIcon.
    Default: ___
  type: ActionIconButtonTypes
    Description: Set the original HTML type of the button (e.g., 'button', 'submit', 'reset').
    Default: "button"
  variant: ActionIconVariants
    Description: Set the ActionIcon variants. Options include 'solid', 'flat', 'outline', 'text'.
    Default: "solid"
  size: ActionIconSizes
    Description: Set the size of the component. 'sm' is equivalent to dense styling. Options: 'sm', 'md', 'lg', 'xl'.
    Default: "md"
  rounded: ActionIconRounded
    Description: Set the border radius of the ActionIcon component. Options: 'sm', 'md', 'lg', 'none', 'full'.
    Default: "md"
  color: ActionIconColors
    Description: Change the ActionIcon color. Options: 'primary', 'secondary', 'danger', etc.
    Default: "primary"
  isLoading: boolean
    Description: Set the loading status of the ActionIcon.
    Default: ___
  disabled: boolean
    Description: Set the disabled state of the ActionIcon.
    Default: ___
  className: string
    Description: Add custom classes for extra styling.
    Default: ___
  ref: Ref<HTMLButtonElement>
    Description: Forward the ref to the underlying button element.
    Default: ___
  ...: ButtonHTMLAttributes | HTMLAttributes
    Description: Native props like 'onClick', 'title', 'aria-label', 'id', etc., are supported.

ActionIconButtonTypes:
  type ActionIconButtonTypes = "button" | "submit" | "reset";

ActionIconVariants:
  type ActionIconVariants = "solid" | "flat" | "outline" | "text";

ActionIconSizes:
  type ActionIconSizes = "sm" | "md" | "lg" | "xl";

ActionIconRounded:
  type ActionIconRounded = "sm" | "md" | "lg" | "none" | "full";

```

### Dropdown with Avatar (React)

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/navigation/dropdown

Illustrates styling the RizzUI Dropdown component with an Avatar element for user-specific actions. This example uses React and the RizzUI Avatar component to display user information.

```javascript
"use client";

import { Dropdown, Text, Avatar } from "rizzui";

export default function App() {
  return (
    <Dropdown placement="bottom-end">
      <Dropdown.Trigger>
        <Avatar
          name="John Doe"
          src="https://randomuser.me/api/portraits/women/40.jpg"
          className="cursor-pointer"
        />
      </Dropdown.Trigger>
      <Dropdown.Menu className="w-56 divide-y text-gray-600">
        <Dropdown.Item className="hover:bg-transparent">
          <Avatar
            name="John Doe"
            src="https://randomuser.me/api/portraits/women/40.jpg"
          />
          <span className="ml-2 text-start">
            <Text className="text-gray-900 font-medium leading-tight">Mary Hoops</Text>
            <Text>maryhe@demo.io</Text>
          </span>
        </Dropdown.Item>
        <div className="mt-3 mb-2 pt-2">
          <Dropdown.Item className="hover:bg-gray-900 hover:text-gray-50">
            Account Settings
          </Dropdown.Item>
          <Dropdown.Item className="hover:bg-gray-900 hover:text-gray-50">Support</Dropdown.Item>
          <Dropdown.Item className="hover:bg-gray-900 hover:text-gray-50">License</Dropdown.Item>
        </div>
        <div className="mt-2 pt-2">
          <Dropdown.Item className="hover:bg-gray-900 hover:text-gray-50">Sign Out</Dropdown.Item>
        </div>
      </Dropdown.Menu>
    </Dropdown>
  );
}

```

### PhoneNumber: Sizes Example

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/integrations/phone-number

Shows how to adjust the vertical size of the PhoneNumber component using the 'size' prop. Options include 'sm', 'default', 'lg', and 'xl' to fit various layout requirements.

```javascript
import PhoneNumber from "@components/phone-number";

export default function App() {
  return (
    <>
      <PhoneNumber label="Phone Number Small" country="us" size="sm" />
      <PhoneNumber label="Phone Number Default" country="us" />
      <PhoneNumber label="Phone Number Large" country="us" size="lg" />
      <PhoneNumber label="Phone Number Extra Large" country="us" size="xl" />
    </>
  );
}
```

### Custom Style Modal Example

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/0.8.7/overlays/modal

Demonstrates how to implement a modal with custom styling using the RizzUI library in a React application. It showcases the use of various RizzUI components like Button, Input, Password, Checkbox, and ActionIcon within a customizable Modal structure.

```react
import { useState } from "react";
import {
  Modal,
  Button,
  Text,
  ActionIcon,
  Input,
  Password,
  Checkbox,
} from "rizzui";
import { XMarkIcon } from "@heroicons/react/20/solid";

export default function App() {
  const [modalState, setModalState] = useState(false);
  return (
    <>
      <Button onClick={() => setModalState(true)}>Custom Style Modal</Button>
      <Modal
        isOpen={modalState}
        onClose={() => setModalState(false)}
        overlayClassName="backdrop-blur"
        containerClassName="!max-w-4xl !shadow-2xl"
      >
        <div className="m-auto px-7 pt-6 pb-8">
          <div className="mb-7 flex items-center justify-between">
            <Text as="h3">Welcome to RizzUI</Text>
            <ActionIcon
              size="sm"
              variant="text"
              onClick={() => setModalState(false)}
            >
              <XMarkIcon className="h-auto w-6" strokeWidth={1.8} />
            </ActionIcon>
          </div>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-y-6 gap-x-5 [&_label>span]:font-medium">
            <Input label="First Name *" inputClassName="border-2" size="lg" />
            <Input label="Last Name *" inputClassName="border-2" size="lg" />
            <Input
              label="Email *"
              inputClassName="border-2"
              size="lg"
              className="col-span-2"
            />
            <Password
              label="Password *"
              inputClassName="border-2"
              size="lg"
              className="col-span-2"
            />
            <Password
              label="Confirm Password *"
              inputClassName="border-2"
              size="lg"
              className="col-span-2"
            />
            <Checkbox
              size="lg"
              inputClassName="border-2"
              className="col-span-2"
              label={
                <Text className="text-sm">
                  I agree to RizzUI&lsquo;s{" "}
                  <a className="underline">Terms of Service</a> and{" "}
                  <a className="underline">Privacy Policy</a>
                </Text>
              }
            />
            <Button
              type="submit"
              size="lg"
              className="col-span-2 mt-2"
              onClick={() => setModalState(false)}
            >
              Create an Account
            </Button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </Modal>
    </>
  );
}
```

```typescript
      </Tab.Panels>
    </Tab>
  );
}
```

### RizzUI Tab Component API Reference

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/0.8.7/navigation/tabs

Comprehensive API documentation for the RizzUI Tab component and its sub-components (Tab.List, Tab.ListItem, Tab.Panels), detailing all available props, their types, descriptions, and default values.

```APIDOC
Tab Component Props:
  vertical: boolean
    - When true, the orientation of the Tab.List will be vertical, otherwise it will be horizontal.
    - Default: ___
  selectedIndex: number
    - The selected index if you want to use the Tab component as a controlled component.
    - Default: ___
  onChange: ((index: number) => void)
    - A function called whenever the active tab changes.
    - Default: ___
  hideHoverAnimation: boolean
    - Use this prop to hide hover animation.
    - Default: false
  children: ReactElement
    - Only allow Tab.List and Tab.Panels as children.
    - Default: ___
  className: string
    - Add classes to the main wrapper of this component.
    - Default: ___

Tab.List Component Props:
  children: ReactElement
    - Only allow Tab.ListItem as children.
    - Default: ___
  className: string
    - Add classes to the Tab.List of this component.
    - Default: ___

Tab.ListItem Component Props:
  children: ReactNode
    - Use any valid React element or string.
    - Default: ___
  className: string
    - Add classes to the Tab.ListItem of this component.
    - Default: ___

Tab.Panels Component Props:
  children: ReactElement
    - Only allow Tab.Panel as children.
    - Default: ___
  className: string
    - Add classes to the Tab.Panels of this component.
    - Default: ___

```

### RizzUI Tooltip API Reference

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/0.8.7/overlays/tooltip

Provides detailed API documentation for the RizzUI Tooltip component, including its available props, their types, default values, and descriptions. It also defines the supported types for placements, children, colors, sizes, and rounded variants.

```APIDOC
Tooltip Props:
  content: ReactNode | Content for tooltip | __
  placement: TooltipPlacements | Supported Tooltip Placements are: | bottom
  children: TooltipChildren | Pass children which will have tooltip | __
  color: TooltipColors | Change Tooltip color | "primary"
  size: TooltipSizes | Supported Tooltip sizes are: | "md"
  rounded: TooltipRounded | The rounded variants are: | "md"
  shadow: TooltipShadows | Supported tooltip shadows are: | "md"
  className: string | Add custom classes to the tooltip container | __
  showArrow: boolean | Whether tooltip arrow should be shown or hidden | true
  arrowClassName: string | Add custom classes to the tooltip arrow | __

Tooltip Placements:
  type TooltipPlacements =
    | "left"
    | "right"
    | "top"
    | "bottom"
    | "left-start"
    | "left-end"
    | "right-start"
    | "right-end";

Tooltip Children:
  type TooltipChildren = Element & { ref?: RefObject<any> | undefined };

Tooltip Colors:
  type TooltipColors =
    | "primary"
    | "invert"
    | "secondary"
    | "danger"
    | "info"
    | "success"
    | "warning"
    | "invert";

Tooltip Sizes:
  type TooltipSizes = "sm" | "md" | "lg" | "xl";

Tooltip Rounded:
  type TooltipRounded = "sm" | "md" | "lg" | "none" | "pill";

Tooltip Shadows:
  type TooltipShadows = "sm" | "md" | "lg" | "none";
```

--------------------------------

### PlaceContentType Definition

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/0.8.7/layouts/grid

Defines the possible values for aligning content within the grid container, affecting both axes. Supports center, start, end, between, around, evenly, and stretch.

```typescript
type PlaceContentType =
  | "center"
  | "start"
  | "end"
  | "between"
  | "around"
  | "evenly"
  | "stretch";
```

### Enable Search in MultiSelect

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/Inputs/multi-select

Explains how to make the MultiSelect component searchable, allowing users to quickly find options within a long list. This example also includes the clearable functionality for easy resetting of selections.

```javascript
"use client";

import { useState } from 'react'
import { MultiSelect } from "rizzui";

const options = [
  { label: "Apple üçé", value: "apple" },
  { label: "Banana üçå", value: "banana" },
  { label: "Cherry üçí", value: "cherry" },
 ...
];

export default function App() {
  const [value, setValue] = useState([]);
  return (
    <MultiSelect
      value={value}
      clearable={true}
      searchable={true}
      options={options}
      onChange={setValue}
      onClear={() => setValue([])}
      label="Multi Select"
    />
  );
}
```

### RizzUI Grid Component API Reference

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/layouts/grid

API documentation for the RizzUI Grid component, detailing its available props for defining grid structure, alignment, and spacing.

```APIDOC
Grid Props:
  as: (string) Render as a specific HTML element (default: 'div').
  columns: (ColumnsType) Defines the number of columns in the grid.
  rows: (RowsType) Defines the number of rows in the grid.
  justify: (JustifyType) Controls the alignment of grid items along the row axis.
  align: (AlignType) Controls the alignment of grid items along the column axis.
  gap: (GapType) Sets the spacing between grid columns and rows (default: '4').
  placeContent: (PlaceContentType) Shorthand for justify-content and align-content.
  placeItems: (PlaceItemsType) Shorthand for justify-items and align-items.
  children: (React.ReactNode) Content to be rendered within the grid.
  className: (string) Custom CSS classes to apply to the grid container.

Note: Other standard HTML attributes like id, title, onClick are also supported.
```

--------------------------------

### RizzUI Tooltip Color Property

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/0.8.7/overlays/tooltip

### RizzUI Alert with Close Button Example

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/feedback/alert

Demonstrates how to implement a closable Alert component in React using the 'closable' and 'onClose' props. It includes state management to control the alert's visibility and a button to trigger its display.

```javascript
import React from "react";
import { Alert, Button } from "rizzui";

export default function App() {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = React.useState(true);
  return (
    <>
      <Button
        color="info"
        onClick={() => setIsOpen(true)}
        className="tracking-wider"
      >
        Info Alert
      </Button>
      {isOpen && (
        <Alert
          color="info"
          variant="flat"
          closable
          onClose={() => setIsOpen(false)}
        >
          <Text className="font-semibold">Alert with info</Text>
          <Text>
            Attention All! We are excited to announce the launch of our new product/service.
          </Text>
        </Alert>
      )}
    </>
  );
}
```

--------------------------------

### Configure RizzUI Drawer Placement and Resizer in React

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/0.8.7/overlays/drawer

Illustrates how to set the placement and enable the resize handler for the RizzUI Drawer component. Examples show 'top', 'bottom', 'left', and 'right' placements, along with enabling 'enableResizer' and setting 'customSize'.

```typescript
import { useState } from "react";
import { Drawer, Button, Text } from "rizzui";

export default function App() {
  const [drawerSate, setDrawerState] = useState({
    isOpen: false,
    placement: "left",
  });
  return (
    <>
      <div className="relative py-5">
        <div className="flex h-72 flex-col items-center justify-between">
          <Button
            variant="outline"
            onClick={() =>
              setDrawerState((prevState) => ({
                ...prevState,
                isOpen: true,
                placement: "top",
              }))
            }
          >
            Top Drawer
          </Button>
          <Button
            variant="outline"
            onClick={() =>
              setDrawerState((prevState) => ({
                ...prevState,
                isOpen: true,
                placement: "bottom",
              }))
            }
          >
            Bottom Drawer
          </Button>
        </div>
        <div className="absolute top-1/2 flex w-full -translate-y-1/2 transform items-center justify-around">
          <Button
            variant="outline"
            onClick={() =>
              setDrawerState((prevState) => ({
                ...prevState,
                isOpen: true,
                placement: "left",
              }))
            }
          >
            Left Drawer
          </Button>
          <Button
            variant="outline"
            onClick={() =>
              setDrawerState((prevState) => ({
                ...prevState,
                isOpen: true,
                placement: "right",
              }))
            }
          >
            Right Drawer
          </Button>
        </div>
      </div>
      <Drawer
        customSize={384}
        enableResizer={true}
        isOpen={drawerSate.isOpen}
        placement={drawerSate.placement}
        onClose={() => setDrawerState((prevState) => ({ ...prevState, isOpen: false }))}
      >
        <div className="py-4 px-5">
          The drawer placement on the{" "}
          <Text as="strong">
            &quot;{drawerSate.placement}&quot;
          </Text>
        </div>
      </Drawer>
    </>
  );
}

```

### PlaceSelfType Definition

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/0.8.7/layouts/grid

Defines the possible values for aligning a single grid item within its grid area, affecting both axes. Supports center, auto, start, end, and stretch.

```typescript
type PlaceSelfType = "center" | "auto" | "start" | "end" | "stretch";
```

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/0.8.7/layouts/grid

```typescript
type JustifyType =
  | "start"
  | "end"
  | "center"
  | "between"
  | "around"
  | "evenly"
  | "stretch";
```

### RizzUI Textarea API Reference

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/Inputs/textarea

Provides a detailed API reference for the RizzUI Textarea component, listing all available props, their types, default values, and descriptions. It also includes references to related type definitions.

```APIDOC
Textarea Props:
  label: ReactNode | Set field label | __
  labelWeight: LabelWeight | Set label font weight | "medium"
  variant: TextareaVariants | The variants of the component are: | "outline"
  size: TextareaSizes | The size of the component. "sm" is equivalent to the dense input styling. | "md"
  rounded: TextareaRounded | The rounded variants are: | "md"
  children: ReactNode | Default value in textarea | __
  cols: number | Set custom cols | __
  rows: number | Set custom rows | 5
  placeholder: string |  | __
  disabled: boolean | Whether the textarea is disabled | __
  error: string | Show error message using this prop | __
  helperText: ReactNode | Add helper text. It could be string or a React component | __
  clearable: boolean | add clearable option | __
  onClear: TextareaOnclear | clear event | __
  renderCharacterCount: TextareaRenderCharacterCount | Use this prop to show character count limit | __
  labelClassName: string | Use labelClassName prop to do some addition style for the label | __
  textareaClassName: string | Add custom classes for the input filed extra style | __
  helperClassName: string | This prop allows you to customize the helper message style | __
  errorClassName: string | This prop allows you to customize the error message style | __
  className: string | Add custom classes to the root of the component | __
  ref: Ref<HTMLTextAreaElement> |  | __
  ...: TextareaHTMLAttributes | native props like **value**, **onChange**, **onFocus**, **onBlur** ... | __

Textarea Variants:
  type TextareaVariants = "outline" | "flat" | "text";

Label Weight:
  type LabelWeight = "normal" | "medium" | "semibold" | "bold";

Textarea Sizes:
  type TextareaSizes = "sm" | "md" | "lg" | "xl";

Textarea Rounded:
  type TextareaRounded = "sm" | "md" | "lg" | "xl" | "none";

Textarea onClear:
  type TextareaOnclear = (event) => void;

Textarea Render Character Count:
  type TextareaRenderCharacterCount =
    | (({ characterCount, maxLength }: { characterCount?: number; maxLength?: number }) => ReactNode)
    | undefined;
```

--------------------------------

### RizzUI Text Component API

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/0.8.7/typography/text

API documentation for the RizzUI Text component, detailing its props, supported HTML tags, and font weight options. Includes prop types, descriptions, and default values.

```APIDOC
Text Component Props:
  as: [TextTags] | string
    Description: Specifies the HTML tag to render.
    Default: "p"

  title: string
    Description: Sets the `title` attribute, visible on hover for `abbr` tags.
    Appears only when tag is `abbr`.
    Default: ___

  fontWeight: [TitleWeights] | string
    Description: Controls the font weight of the text. Note: `fontWeight='normal'` won't work with `b`, `strong`, and `q` tags.
    Default: "bold"

  className: string
    Description: Add custom classes for extra styling.
    Default: ___

TextTags:
  Type: "p" | "b" | "span" | "strong" | "abbr" | "q" | "del" | "em" | "i" | "kbd" | "mark" | "small" | "sub" | "sup"

TitleWeights:
  Type: "bold" | "normal" | "medium" | "semibold"
```

### RizzUI Input: Quantity Counter Example - React

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/Inputs/input

Shows how to implement a quantity counter functionality using the RizzUI Input component. It utilizes state management and custom suffix buttons with icons to increment or decrement the input value.

```javascript
"use client";

import { useState } from "react";
import { Input } from "rizzui";
import { ChevronUpIcon, ChevronDownIcon } from "@heroicons/react/24/outline";

export default function App() {
  const [state, setState] = useState(0);

  return (
    <Input
      label="Quantity Counter"
      type="number"
      min={0}
      step={1}
      value={state}
      onChange={(e) => setState(Number(e.target.value))}
      suffix={
        <div className="-mr-3.5 grid gap-[2px] p-0.5 rtl:-ml-3.5 rtl:-mr-0">
          <button
            type="button"
            className="rounded-[3px] bg-gray-100 py-0.5 px-1.5 hover:bg-gray-200 focus:bg-gray-200"
            onClick={() => setState((prevState) => prevState + 1)}
          >
            <ChevronUpIcon className="h-3 w-3" />
          </button>
          <button
            type="button"
            className="rounded-[3px] bg-gray-100 py-0.5 px-1.5 hover:bg-gray-200 focus:bg-gray-200"
            onClick={() => setState((prevState) => prevState - 1)}
          >
            <ChevronDownIcon className="h-3 w-3" />
          </button>
        </div>
      }
    />
  );
}
```

--------------------------------

### React Hook Form Submission Example

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/integrations/react-hook-form

Demonstrates a form submission using React Hook Form, including input fields and a submit button. It utilizes a custom Select component likely powered by React Hook Form's controller.

```javascript
function MyForm() {
  // Assume useForm is imported from 'react-hook-form'
  // Assume SelectComponent is a custom component that works with RHF
  const { register, handleSubmit, control } = useForm();

  const onSubmit = (data) => {
    console.log(data);
  };

  const companyOptions = [
    { value: '1', label: 'Company A' },
    { value: '2', label: 'Company B' },
  ];

  return (
    <div>
      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit(onSubmit)}>
        {/* Example using a custom Select component with RHF Controller */}
        <Controller
          name="company"
          control={control}
          rules={{ required: 'Company is required' }}
          render={({ field }) => (
            <SelectComponent
              {...field}
              options={companyOptions}
              placeholder="Select Company"
              value={companyOptions?.find((r) => r.value === field.value)} 
              onChange={(selectedOption) => field.onChange(selectedOption.value)}
            />
          )}
        />

        <Button
          type="submit"
          className="w-full mt-2"
        >
          Submit
        </Button>
      </form>
    </div>
  );
}
```

### Custom Size Modal with RizzUI

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/overlays/modal

Demonstrates how to use the `customSize` property of the RizzUI `Modal` component to set a specific width for the modal. This example shows a modal with a width of '1080px' and includes form elements for user input.

```javascript
"use client";

import { useState } from "react";
import {
  Modal,
  Button,
  Title,
  Text,
  ActionIcon,
  Input,
  Password,
  Checkbox,
} from "rizzui";
import { XMarkIcon } from "@heroicons/react/20/solid";

export default function App() {
  const [modalState, setModalState] = useState(false);
  return (
    <>
      <Button onClick={() => setModalState(true)}>Custom Size Modal</Button>
      <Modal
        isOpen={modalState}
        onClose={() => setModalState(false)}
        customSize="1080px"
      >
        <div className="m-auto px-7 pt-6 pb-8">
          <div className="mb-7 flex items-center justify-between">
            <Title as="h3">Welcome to RizzUI</Title>
            <ActionIcon
              size="sm"
              variant="text"
              onClick={() => setModalState(false)}
            >
              <XMarkIcon className="h-auto w-6" strokeWidth={1.8} />
            </ActionIcon>
          </div>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-y-6 gap-x-5 [&_label>span]:font-medium">
            <Input label="First Name *" inputClassName="border-2" size="lg" />
            <Input label="Last Name *" inputClassName="border-2" size="lg" />
            <Input
              label="Email *"
              inputClassName="border-2"
              size="lg"
              className="col-span-2"
            />
            <Password
              label="Password *"
              inputClassName="border-2"
              size="lg"
              className="col-span-2"
            />
            <Password
              label="Confirm Password *"
              inputClassName="border-2"
              size="lg"
              className="col-span-2"
            />
            <Checkbox
              size="lg"
              inputClassName="border-2"
              className="col-span-2"
              label={
                <Text className="text-sm">
                  I agree to RizzUI&lsquo;s{" "}
                  <a className="underline">Terms of Service</a> and{" "}
                  <a className="underline">Privacy Policy</a>
                </Text>
              }
            />
            <Button
              type="submit"
              size="lg"
              className="col-span-2 mt-2"
              onClick={() => setModalState(false)}
            >
              Create an Account
            </Button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </Modal>
    </>
  );
}

```

### RizzUI Popover Component API Reference

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/overlays/popover

Provides detailed API documentation for the RizzUI Popover component, outlining all available props, their types, descriptions, and default values. It also includes references to related type definitions for sizes, rounded variants, placements, shadows, and animations.

```APIDOC
Popover Props:
  children: Use **Popover.Trigger** & **Popover.Content** as childrens
  gap: number - Set the offset value from **Popover.Trigger** to **Popover.Content**. Default: "8"
  isOpen: boolean - Pass **isOpen** state to toggle the popover content
  setIsOpen: Dispatch<SetStateAction<boolean>> - Pass **setIsOpen** to set open value
  size: [PopoverSizes](#popover-sizes) - Supported popover sizes are: "sm" | "md" | "lg" | "xl". Default: "md"
  rounded: [PopoverRounded](#popover-rounded) - The rounded variants are: "sm" | "md" | "lg" | "none" | "pill". Default: "md"
  placement: [PopoverPlacements](#popover-placements) - Supported popover placements are: "bottom". Default: "bottom"
  shadow: [PopoverShadow](#popover-shadows) - Supported popover shadows are: "md". Default: "md"
  animation: [PopoverAnimation](#popover-animations) - Supported popover animations are: "zoomIn". Default: "zoomIn"
  showArrow: boolean - Whether popover arrow should be shown or hidden. Default: "true"
  arrowClassName: string - Add custom classes to the arrow
  enableOverlay: boolean - Whether popover backdrop overlay should be shown or hidden. Default: "false"
  overlayClassName: string - Add custom classes to the overlay

Popover Sizes:
  type PopoverSizes = "sm" | "md" | "lg" | "xl";

Popover Rounded:
  type PopoverRounded = "sm" | "md" | "lg" | "none" | "pill";

```

### RizzUI Input: Clearable Button Example (React)

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/Inputs/input

Shows how to make the RizzUI Input component clearable by setting the 'clearable' prop to true. The 'onClear' prop handles the logic for clearing the input's value.

```javascript
"use client";

import { useState } from "react";
import { Input } from "rizzui";

export default function App() {
  const [state, setState] = useState("This is Jhon.");

  return (
    <Input
      type="text"
      label="Name"
      value={state}
      placeholder="clearable ..."
      onChange={(e) => setState(e.target.value)}
      onClear={() => setState("")}
      clearable
    />
  );
}

```

```APIDOC
RadialProgressBar Props:

  value: number
    Percentage of filled bar
    Default: ___

  size: number

    Default: 100

  trackColor: string
    Color of the track of the RadialProgressBar
    Default: #f0f0f0

  progressColor: string
    Color of the progress of the RadialProgressBar
    Default: #111111

  progressbarWidth: number
    Width of the progress bar
    Default: 8

  gradientColor: string
    Gradient color of the progress of the RadialProgressBar
    Default: ___

  gradientId: string
    Unique id for the gradient color stop
    Default: ___

  startAngle: ProgressbarStartAngles
    Start angle of the RadialProgressBar
    Default: 90

  trackClassName: string
    Overrides the default style of RadialProgressBar track
    Default: ___

  progressBarClassName: string
    Overrides the default style of RadialProgressBar progress
    Default: ___

  useParentResponsive: boolean
    Uses the parent components width height for responsive
    Default: false

Progressbar Start Angles:

  type ProgressbarStartAngles = 0 | 45 | 90 | 180 | 270 | 360;
```

### Progressbar API Reference

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/feedback/progressbar

Comprehensive API documentation for the RizzUI Progressbar component, detailing all available props, their types, descriptions, default values, and related type definitions for sizes, rounded variants, colors, and label positions.

```APIDOC
Progressbar Props:
  value: number
    - Percentage of filled bar.
    - Default: ___

  label: string
    - Pass label to show percentage inside bar. It will only work when size="xl".
    - Default: ""

  variant: "solid" | "flat"
    - The variants of the components are:
    - Default: "solid"

  size: ProgressbarSize
    - Size of the components are:
    - Default: "md"

  rounded: ProgressbarRounded
    - The rounded variants are:
    - Default: "pill"

  color: ProgressbarColor
    - Pass color variations
    - Default: "primary"

  labelPosition: ProgressbarLabelPosition
    - Sets the label position of progressbar component
    - Default: "inlineRight"

  className: string
    - To style the root of the component
    - Default: ___

  barClassName: string
    - To style bar of the component
    - Default: ___

  trackClassName: string
    - To style progressbar track of the component
    - Default: ___

  labelClassName: string
    - To style label
    - Default: ___

ProgressbarSize Type:
  "sm" | "md" | "lg" | "xl"

ProgressbarRounded Type:
  "sm" | "md" | "lg" | "pill" | "none"

ProgressbarColor Type:
  "primary" | "secondary" | "danger" | "info" | "success" | "warning"

ProgressbarLabelPosition Type:
  "inlineLeft" | "inlineRight" | "insideBar"
```

### RizzUI Accordion API Reference

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/0.8.7/data-display/accordion

Comprehensive API documentation for the RizzUI Accordion component, detailing props for the main Accordion, Accordion.Header, and Accordion.Body sub-components, including their types, descriptions, and default values.

```APIDOC
Accordion Component API:

Accordion Props:
  as: (string) Set HTML tag of the Accordion. Either 'div' or 'li'. Use 'li' when you are building collapse navigation menu. Default: "div"
  duration: (number) Set transition duration. Default: __
  defaultOpen: (boolean) Initial active panel. Default: false
  children: (ReactNode) Note: Use only Accordion.Header & Accordion.Body as a child component. Default: __
  className: (string) Add custom classes to the Accordion component for extra style. Default: __

Accordion.Header Props:
  ref: (useRef) Use ref prop to access DOM nodes of Accordion.Header. Default: __
  children: (ReactNode | ({ open }: { open: boolean }) => React.ReactNode) Use render props to animate chevron icon. Default: __
  className: (string) Add custom classes to the Accordion.Header component for extra style. Default: __

Accordion.Body Props:
  ref: (useRef) Use ref prop to access DOM nodes of Accordion.Body. Default: __
  as: (string) Set HTML tag of the Accordion. Either 'div' or 'li'. Use 'li' when you are building collapse navigation menu. Default: "div"
  children: (ReactNode) Use any valid ReactElement or text. Default: __
  className: (string) Add custom classes to the Accordion.Body component for extra style. Default: __

```

### Box Component API Reference

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/layouts/box

Provides detailed API documentation for the RizzUI Box component, including its available props, their types, descriptions, and default values. It also notes that standard HTML element props are inherited.

```APIDOC
Box Props:
  as: string | React.ElementType
    Description: Specifies the HTML element or component to render the Box as. Defaults to 'div'.
    Default: "div"

  children: React.ReactNode
    Description: Accepts any renderable React content, including other components, text, or elements.
    Default: ___

  className: string
    Description: Allows adding custom CSS classes to the Box component for styling purposes.
    Default: ___

  Inherited Props:
    Description: The Box component also accepts all standard HTML element attributes and event handlers (e.g., id, title, onClick, style) as props, which are passed directly to the underlying HTML element.
    Examples: id, title, onClick, style, data-testid
```

### RizzUI Switch API Reference

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/Inputs/switch

Provides a detailed API reference for the RizzUI Switch component, outlining all available props, their types, descriptions, default values, and related types for variants and sizes.

```APIDOC
Switch Props:
  label: ReactNode | Set field label | __
  labelWeight: LabelWeight | Set label font weight | "medium"
  labelPlacement: "left" | "right" | Change label direction | "right"
  variant: SwitchVariants | The variants of the component are: | "flat"
  size: SwitchSizes | The size of the component. | "md"
  rounded: SwitchRounded | The rounded variants are: | "pill"
  disabled: boolean | Whether the switch is disabled | false
  onIcon: ReactNode | Set custom icon when the switch is on | __
  offIcon: ReactNode | Set custom icon when the switch is off | __
  helperText: ReactNode | Add helper text. It could be string or a React component | __
  error: string | Show error message using this prop | __
  labelClassName: string | Override default CSS style of label | __
  switchClassName: string | Override default CSS style of switch | __
  switchKnobClassName: string | Override default CSS style of switch knob | __
  helperClassName: string | Override default CSS style of helperText | __
  errorClassName: string | Override default CSS style of error message | __
  className: string | Add custom classes to the root of the component | __
  ref: Ref<HTMLInputElement> |  | __
  ...: InputHTMLAttributes | native props like **value**, **onChange**, **onFocus**, **onBlur** ... | __

Switch Variants:
  type SwitchVariants = "outline" | "flat";

Label Weight:
  type LabelWeight = "normal" | "medium" | "semibold" | "bold";

Switch Sizes:
  type SwitchSizes = "sm" | "md" | "lg" | "xl";

Switch Rounded:
  type SwitchRounded = "none" | "sm" | "md" | "lg" | "full";
```

```APIDOC
PinCode Props:

    - Default: true
  placeholder: `string`
    - Set placeholder text
    - Default: "o"
  variant: [PincodeVariants](#pincode-variants)
    - The variants of the component are:
    - Default: "outline"

    - The size of the component. "sm" is equivalent to the dense input styling.
    - Default: "md"
  rounded: [PincodeRounded](#pincode-rounded)
    - The rounded variants are:
    - Default: "md"
  error: `string`
    - Show error message using this prop
    - Default: __
  inputClassName: `string`
    - Add custom classes for the input filed extra style
    - Default: __
  errorClassName: `string`
    - This prop allows you to customize the error message style
    - Default: __
  className: `string`
    - Add custom classes to the root of the component
    - Default: __

PincodeSetvalue Type:
  type PincodeSetvalue = Dispatch<SetStateAction<string | number | undefined>>;

PincodeVariants Type:
  type PincodeVariants = "outline" | "flat";

PincodeSizes Type:
  type PincodeSizes = "sm" | "md" | "lg" | "xl";

PincodeRounded Type:
```

### Functional Stepper with Navigation (React)

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/navigation/stepper

Provides an example of a functional Stepper component that can be controlled by navigation buttons. It uses React's `useState` hook to manage the `currentStep` and includes 'Next' and 'Reset' buttons to change the active step.

```javascript
"use client";

import React from "react";
import { Stepper, Button } from "rizzui";

export default function App() {
  const [currentStep, setCurrentStep] = React.useState(0);
  return (
    <>
      <Stepper currentIndex={currentStep}>
        <Stepper.Step title="Step 1" description="This is a description" />
        <Stepper.Step title="Step 2" description="This is a description" />
        <Stepper.Step title="Step 3" description="This is a description" />
      </Stepper>

      <div className="mt-7 flex space-x-4">
        <Button
          disabled={currentStep === 3}
          onClick={() => setCurrentStep(currentStep + 1)}
        >
          Next
        </Button>

        {currentStep === 3 && (
          <Button onClick={() => setCurrentStep(0)}>Reset</Button>
        )}
      </div>
    </>
  );
}
```

### Dropdown Component API Reference

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/navigation/dropdown

Provides detailed API documentation for the RizzUI Dropdown component, outlining all available props, their types, descriptions, and default values for customization.

```APIDOC
Dropdown Props:

  children: __
    Description: Use **Dropdown.Trigger** & **Dropdown.Menu** as childrens.
    Type: __
    Default: __

  rounded: [DropdownRounded](#dropdown-rounded)
    Description: The rounded variants supported by this component.
    Type: [DropdownRounded](#dropdown-rounded)
    Default: "md"

  shadow: [DropdownShadows](#dropdown-shadows)
    Description: The shadow variants supported by this component.
    Type: [DropdownShadows](#dropdown-shadows)
    Default: "md"

  placement: [DropdownPlacement](#dropdown-placement)
    Description: The dropdown menu placements. Won't work if **inPortal** prop is false.
    Type: [DropdownPlacement](#dropdown-placement)
    Default: "bottom-start"

  inPortal: boolean
    Description: Whether the **Dropdown.Menu** is rendered on the portal or not.
    Type: boolean
    Default: "true"

  modal: boolean
    Description: Whether the body scrollbar is hidden or not when dropdown is visible.
    Type: boolean
    Default: "false"

  gap: number
    Description: Sets the gap between trigger and dropdown if portal is true.
    Type: number
    Default: "6"

  className: string
    Description: Add classes to the main wrapper of this component.
    Type: string
    Default: __
```

### AdvancedRadio Component API

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/0.8.7/Inputs/advanced-radio

Comprehensive API documentation for the RizzUI AdvancedRadio component. It details available props, their types, descriptions, default values, and related type definitions for sizes and rounded variants. The component accepts all native input HTML attributes.

```APIDOC
AdvancedRadio Props:
  children: ReactNode
    - Description: Pass content as children to the radio button.
    - Default: ___
  disabled: boolean
    - Description: Whether the radio button is disabled.
    - Default: ___
  size: RadioSizes
    - Description: The size of the component. "sm" is equivalent to dense input styling.
    - Type: [RadioSizes](#advanced-radio-sizes)
    - Default: "md"
  rounded: RadioRounded
    - Description: The rounded variants available for the component.
    - Type: [RadioRounded](#advanced-radio-rounded)
    - Default: "md"
  inputClassName: string
    - Description: Add custom classes to style the input element itself.
    - Default: ___
  contentClassName: string
    - Description: Add custom classes to style the content wrapper of the radio button.
    - Default: ___
  className: string
    - Description: Add custom classes to the root element of the component.
    - Default: ___
  ref: Ref<HTMLInputElement>
    - Description: A ref to the underlying HTML input element.
    - Default: ___
  ...InputHTMLAttributes: InputHTMLAttributes
    - Description: Accepts native HTML input attributes such as value, onChange, onFocus, onBlur, etc.
    - Default: ___

Related Types:

RadioSizes:
  type RadioSizes = "sm" | "md" | "lg" | "xl";

RadioRounded:
  type RadioRounded = "sm" | "md" | "lg" | "pill" | "none";
```

### RizzUI Input Component API Reference

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/0.8.7/Inputs/input

This section details the props available for the RizzUI Input component. It covers standard HTML input attributes and component-specific configurations for customization, including type, label, variants, sizing, and styling.

```APIDOC
Input Component Props:

- type: [InputTypes](#input-types) | Specifies the input field's type (e.g., text, number, email). Defaults to "text".
- label: ReactNode | Sets the label for the input field.
- labelWeight: [LabelWeight](#label-weight) | Controls the font weight of the label. Defaults to "medium".
- variant: [InputVariants](#input-variants) | Defines the visual style of the input field (e.g., outline, flat, text). Defaults to "outline".
- size: [InputSizes](#input-sizes) | Determines the size of the input component. "sm" provides dense styling. Defaults to "md".
- rounded: [InputRounded](#input-rounded) | Sets the border radius of the input field. Defaults to "md".
- placeholder: string | Placeholder text displayed in the input field.
- disabled: boolean | Disables the input field if true.
- clearable: boolean | Adds a button to clear the input content if true.
- onClear: [InputOnclear](#input-onclear) | Callback function triggered when the clear button is activated.
- prefix: ReactNode | Content displayed at the start of the input field (e.g., an icon).
- suffix: ReactNode | Content displayed at the end of the input field (e.g., an icon).
- helperText: ReactNode | Additional text displayed below the input field for guidance.
- error: string | Displays an error message if provided.
- labelClassName: string | Custom CSS class for the label element.
- inputClassName: string | Custom CSS class for the input element itself.
- prefixClassName: string | Custom CSS class for the prefix element.
- suffixClassName: string | Custom CSS class for the suffix element.
- helperClassName: string | Custom CSS class for the helper text element.
- errorClassName: string | Custom CSS class for the error message element.
- className: string | Custom CSS class applied to the root element of the component.
- ref: Ref<HTMLInputElement> | A ref to the underlying HTML input element.
- ...InputHTMLAttributes: object | Accepts native HTML input attributes like value, onChange, onFocus, onBlur, etc.
```

```APIDOC
Input Type Definitions:

InputTypes:
  | "text"
  | "number"
  | "email"
  | "time"
  | "date"
  | "datetime-local"
  | "month"
  | "search"
  | "tel"
  | "url"
  | "week";

LabelWeight:
  | "normal"
  | "medium"
  | "semibold"
  | "bold";

InputVariants:
  | "outline"
  | "flat"
  | "text";

InputSizes:
  | "sm"
  | "md"
  | "lg"
  | "xl";

InputRounded:
  | "sm"
  | "md"
  | "lg"
  | "none"
  | "pill";

InputOnclear:
  (event) => void;
```

### RizzUI Tab Component API Reference

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/navigation/tabs

Provides detailed API documentation for the RizzUI `Tab` component and its sub-components (`Tab.List`, `Tab.ListItem`, `Tab.Panels`, `Tab.Panel`). It outlines available props, their types, descriptions, and default values, enabling full customization.

```APIDOC
Tab Component Props:
  vertical: boolean
    - When true, the orientation of the Tab.List will be vertical, otherwise it will be horizontal.
    - Default: undefined
  selectedIndex: number
    - The selected index if you want to use the Tab component as a controlled component.
    - Default: undefined
  onChange: ((index: number) => void)
    - A function called whenever the active tab changes.
    - Default: undefined
  hideHoverAnimation: boolean
    - Use this prop to hide hover animation.
    - Default: false
  children: ReactElement
    - Only allow Tab.List and Tab.Panels as children.
    - Default: undefined
  className: string
    - Add classes to the main wrapper of this component.
    - Default: undefined

Tab.List Component Props:
  children: ReactElement
    - Only allow Tab.ListItem as children.
    - Default: undefined
  className: string
    - Add classes to the Tab.List of this component.
    - Default: undefined

Tab.ListItem Component Props:
  children: ReactNode
    - Use any valid React element or string.
    - Default: undefined
  className: string
    - Add classes to the Tab.ListItem of this component.
    - Default: undefined

Tab.Panels Component Props:
  children: ReactElement
    - Only allow Tab.Panel as children.
    - Default: undefined
  className: string
    - Add classes to the Tab.Panels of this component.
    - Default: undefined

Tab.Panel Component Props:
  children: ReactNode
    - Use any valid React element or string.
    - Default: undefined
  className: string
    - Add classes to the Tab.Panel of this component.
    - Default: undefined
```

### Custom Size Modal Example

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/0.8.7/overlays/modal

This React component demonstrates how to set a custom width for the RizzUI Modal using the `customSize` prop. It imports necessary components from 'react' and 'rizzui', manages modal visibility with `useState`, and applies a width of '1080px' to the Modal component.

```javascript
import { useState } from "react";
import {
  Modal,
  Button,
  Text,
  ActionIcon,
  Input,
  Password,
  Checkbox,
} from "rizzui";
import { XMarkIcon } from "@heroicons/react/20/solid";

export default function App() {
  const [modalState, setModalState] = useState(false);
  return (
    <>
      <Button onClick={() => setModalState(true)}>Custom Size Modal</Button>
      <Modal
        isOpen={modalState}
        onClose={() => setModalState(false)}
        customSize="1080px"
      >
        <div className="m-auto px-7 pt-6 pb-8">
          <div className="mb-7 flex items-center justify-between">
            <Text as="h3">Welcome to RizzUI</Text>
            <ActionIcon
              size="sm"
              variant="text"
              onClick={() => setModalState(false)}
            >
              <XMarkIcon className="h-auto w-6" strokeWidth={1.8} />
            </ActionIcon>
          </div>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-y-6 gap-x-5 [&_label>span]:font-medium">
            <Input label="First Name *" inputClassName="border-2" size="lg" />
            <Input label="Last Name *" inputClassName="border-2" size="lg" />
            <Input
              label="Email *"
              inputClassName="border-2"
              size="lg"
              className="col-span-2"
            />
            <Password
              label="Password *"
              inputClassName="border-2"
              size="lg"
              className="col-span-2"
            />
            <Password
              label="Confirm Password *"
              inputClassName="border-2"
              size="lg"
              className="col-span-2"
            />
            <Checkbox
              size="lg"
              inputClassName="border-2"
              className="col-span-2"
              label={
                <Text className="text-sm">
                  I agree to RizzUI&lsquo;s{" "}
                  <a className="underline">Terms of Service</a> and{" "}
                  <a className="underline">Privacy Policy</a>
                </Text>
              }
            />
            <Button
              type="submit"
              size="lg"
              className="col-span-2 mt-2"
              onClick={() => setModalState(false)}
            >
              Create an Account
            </Button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </Modal>
    </>
  );
}

```

### RizzUI Progressbar Component API Reference

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/0.8.7/feedback/progressbar

Provides detailed API documentation for the RizzUI Progressbar component, outlining all available props, their types, descriptions, and default values. This includes properties for value, label, variant, size, roundedness, color, and styling.

```APIDOC
Progressbar Props:

- value (number): Percentage of filled bar. No default specified.
- label (string): Pass label to show percentage inside bar. It will only work when size="xl". Default: ""
- variant (solid | flat): The variants of the components. Default: "solid"
- size ([ProgressbarSize](#progressbar-sizes)): Size of the component. Default: "md"
- rounded ([ProgressbarRounded](#progressbar-rounded)): The rounded variants. Default: "pill"
- color ([ProgressbarColor](#progressbar-colors)): Pass color variations. Default: "primary"
- labelPosition ([ProgressbarLabelPosition](#progressbar-label-position)): Sets the label position of progressbar component. Default: "inlineRight"
- className (string): To style the root of the component. No default specified.
- barClassName (string): To style bar of the component. No default specified.
- trackClassName (string): To style progressbar track of the component. No default specified.
- labelClassName (string): To style label. No default specified.
```

### Credit Card Input With Gap (React)

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/Inputs/number-input

Implements credit card input fields with visual gaps using RizzUI's NumberInput and pattern formatting. It includes examples for a full card number, expiry date, and CVV, leveraging custom formatting logic for validation and display.

```typescript
"use client";

import { NumberInput, Input, usePatternFormat, NumberInputProps } from "rizzui";

type CardExpiryType = NumberInputProps & {
  isMask?: boolean;
};

export default function App() {
  function CardExpiry({ isMask = false, ...props }: CardExpiryType) {
    const { format } = usePatternFormat({
      ...props,
      format: "##/##",
    });
    const _format = (val: string) => {
      let month = val.substring(0, 2);
      const year = val.substring(2, 4);

      if (month.length === 1 && parseInt(month[0]) > 1) {
        month = `0${month[0]}`;
      } else if (month.length === 2) {
        if (Number(month) === 0) {
          month = "01";
        } else if (Number(month) > 12) {
          month = "12";
        }
      }
      return isMask ? format(`${month}${year}`) : `${month}/${year}`;
    };
    return <NumberInput {...props} format={_format} />;
  }

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
      <NumberInput
        formatType="pattern"
        format="#### #### #### ####"
        value="411111"
        mask="_"
        customInput={Input as React.ComponentType<unknown>}
        {...{ label: "Outline", variant: "outline" }}
      />
      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
        <CardExpiry
          isMask
          formatType="custom"
          placeholder="MM/YY"
          mask={["M", "M", "Y", "Y"]}
          allowEmptyFormatting
          customInput={Input as React.ComponentType<unknown>}
          {...{ variant: "outline" }}
        />
        <NumberInput
          formatType="pattern"
          format="###"
          mask={["C", "V", "V"]}
          allowEmptyFormatting
          customInput={Input as React.ComponentType<unknown>}
          {...{ variant: "outline" }}
        />
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

```

### Format Credit Card and Expiry with RizzUI NumberInput

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/0.8.7/Inputs/number-input

This example demonstrates advanced formatting for credit card inputs using RizzUI's NumberInput. It includes formatting for the main card number with gaps, a custom component for expiry dates (MM/YY) with validation, and a CVC input.

```typescript
import { NumberInput, Input, usePatternFormat, NumberInputProps } from "rizzui";

type CardExpiryType = NumberInputProps & {
  isMask?: boolean;
};

export default function App() {
  function CardExpiry({ isMask = false, ...props }: CardExpiryType) {
    const { format } = usePatternFormat({
      ...props,
      format: "##/##",
    });
    const _format = (val: string) => {
      let month = val.substring(0, 2);
      const year = val.substring(2, 4);

      if (month.length === 1 && parseInt(month[0]) > 1) {
        month = `0${month[0]}`;
      } else if (month.length === 2) {
        if (Number(month) === 0) {
          month = "01";
        } else if (Number(month) > 12) {
          month = "12";
        }
      }
      return isMask ? format(`${month}${year}`) : `${month}/${year}`;
    };
    return <NumberInput {...props} format={_format} />;
  }

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
      <NumberInput
        formatType="pattern"
        format="#### #### #### ####"
        value="411111"
        mask="_"
        customInput={Input as React.ComponentType<unknown>}
        {...{ label: "Outline", variant: "outline" }}
      />
      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
        <CardExpiry
          isMask
          formatType="custom"
          placeholder="MM/YY"
          mask={["M", "M", "Y", "Y"]}
          allowEmptyFormatting
          customInput={Input as React.ComponentType<unknown>}
          {...{ variant: "outline" }}
        />
        <NumberInput
          formatType="pattern"
          format="###"
          mask={["C", "V", "C"]}
          allowEmptyFormatting
          customInput={Input as React.ComponentType<unknown>}
          {...{ variant: "outline" }}
        />
      </div>
    </div>
  );
```

### RizzUI Badge: Icon Integration for Counters (React)

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/data-display/badge

Shows how to use the RizzUI Badge component as a notification counter, typically positioned over an icon. This example demonstrates placing badges with different counts and colors on shopping bag and cart icons.

```react
import { Badge } from "rizzui";
import { ShoppingBagIcon, ShoppingCartIcon } from "@heroicons/react/24/outline";

export default function App() {
  return (
    <>
      <div className="relative inline-flex">
        <ShoppingBagIcon
          className="h-auto w-8"
          strokeWidth={1.2}
        />
        <Badge
          size="sm"
          enableOutlineRing
          className="absolute right-0 top-0 -translate-y-1/3 translate-x-1/2"
        >
          99
        </Badge>
      </div>
      <div className="relative ml-3 inline-flex">
        <ShoppingCartIcon
          className="h-auto w-8"
          strokeWidth={1.2}
        />
        <Badge
          size="sm"
          color="success"
          enableOutlineRing
          className="absolute right-0 top-0 -translate-y-1/3 translate-x-1/2"
        >
          99+
        </Badge>
      </div>

        >
          999+
        </Badge>
      </div>
    </>
  );
}
```

### RizzUI Input Component API Reference

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/Inputs/input

Provides a detailed API reference for the RizzUI Input component, outlining all available props, their types, descriptions, default values, and any associated types or enums.

```APIDOC
Input Props:
  type: [InputTypes](#input-types) | This Input component only support these types | "text"
  label: ReactNode | Set field label | __
  labelWeight: [LabelWeight](#label-weight) | Set label font weight | "medium"
  variant: [InputVariants](#input-variants) | The variants of the component are: | "outline"
  size: [InputSizes](#input-sizes) | The size of the component. "sm" is equivalent to the dense input styling. | "md"
  rounded: [InputRounded](#input-rounded) | The rounded variants are: | "md"
  placeholder: string | Set input placeholder text | __
  disabled: boolean | Whether the input is disabled or not | __
  clearable: boolean | Add clearable option | __
  onClear: [InputOnclear](#input-onclear) | clear event | __
  prefix: ReactNode | The prefix is design for adding any icon or text on the Input field's start (it's a left icon for the `ltr` and right icon for the `rtl`) | __
  suffix: ReactNode | The suffix is design for adding any icon or text on the Input field's end (it's a right icon for the `ltr` and left icon for the `rtl`) | __
  helperText: ReactNode | Add helper text. It could be string or a React component | __
  error: string | Show error message using this prop | __
  labelClassName: string | Override default CSS style of label | __
  inputClassName: string | Override default CSS style of input | __
  prefixClassName: string | Override default CSS style of prefix | __
  suffixClassName: string | Override default CSS style of suffix | __
  helperClassName: string | Override default CSS style of helperText | __
  errorClassName: string | Override default CSS style of error message | __
  className: string | Add custom classes to the root of the component | __
  ref: Ref<HTMLInputElement> |  | __
  ...: InputHTMLAttributes | native props like **value**, **onChange**, **onFocus**, **onBlur** ... | __

Input Types:
  type InputTypes =
  | "text"
  | "number"
  | "email"
  | "time"
  | "date"
  | "datetime-local"
  | "month"
  | "search"
  | "tel"
  | "url"
  | "week";

```

--------------------------------

### Credit Card Input Without Gap (React)

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/Inputs/number-input

Demonstrates credit card input fields without visual gaps, achieved by applying specific CSS classes to RizzUI's NumberInput components. This example also includes custom formatting for expiry dates and CVV inputs.

```typescript
"use client";

import { NumberInput, Input, usePatternFormat, NumberInputProps } from "rizzui";

type CardExpiryType = NumberInputProps & {
  isMask?: boolean;
};

function CardExpiry({ isMask = false, ...props }: CardExpiryType) {
  const { format } = usePatternFormat({
    ...props,
    format: "##/##",
  });
  const _format = (val: string) => {
    let month = val.substring(0, 2);
    const year = val.substring(2, 4);

    if (month.length === 1 && parseInt(month[0]) > 1) {
      month = `0${month[0]}`;
    } else if (month.length === 2) {
      if (Number(month) === 0) {
        month = "01";
      } else if (Number(month) > 12) {
        month = "12";
      }
    }
    return isMask ? format(`${month}${year}`) : `${month}/${year}`;
  };
  return <NumberInput {...props} format={_format} />;
}

export default function App() {
  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col">
      <NumberInput
        formatType="pattern"
        format="#### #### #### ####"
        value="411111"
        mask="_"
        customInput={Input as React.ComponentType<unknown>}
        {...{
          label: "Outline",
          variant: "outline",
          inputClassName:
            "border-b-0 rounded-b-none hover:border-b hover:rounded-b focus:border-b focus:rounded-b",
        }}
      />
      <div className="grid grid-cols-2">
        <CardExpiry
          isMask
          formatType="custom"
          placeholder="MM/YY"
          mask={["M", "M", "Y", "Y"]}
          allowEmptyFormatting
          customInput={Input as React.ComponentType<unknown>}
          {...{
            variant: "outline",
            inputClassName:
              "rounded-t-none rounded-br-none hover:rounded-t hover:rounded-br focus:rounded-t focus:rounded-br",
          }}
        />
        <NumberInput
          formatType="pattern"
          format="###"
          mask={["C", "V", "V"]}
          allowEmptyFormatting
          customInput={Input as React.ComponentType<unknown>}
          {...{
            variant: "outline",
            inputClassName:
              "rounded-t-none rounded-bl-none border-l-0 hover:rounded-t hover:rounded-bl hover:border-l focus:rounded-t focus:rounded-bl focus:border-l",
          }}
        />
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

```

### Box Component API Reference

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/0.8.7/layouts/box

API documentation for the RizzUI Box component, detailing its available props, their types, descriptions, and default values. It also inherits standard HTML element attributes.

```APIDOC
Box Props:
  as: string | React.ElementType - Specifies the HTML element to render the Box as. Defaults to 'div'.
  children: React.ReactNode - Content to be rendered inside the Box component.
  className: string - Allows adding custom CSS classes to the Box component for styling.

  Inherited Props:
  The Box component also accepts all standard HTML element attributes (e.g., id, title, onClick, style, etc.) as props.
```

### React Datepicker: Clearable Range Datepicker

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/integrations/react-datepicker

Demonstrates a date range picker with a clearable input. It allows users to select a start and end date, displays two months at once, and provides a clear button for resetting the selection.

```javascript
import { ReactDatePicker } from "@components/datepicker";

export default function App() {
  const [starDate, setStartDate] = React.useState<[Date | null, Date | null]>();
  return (
    <div className="h-96">
      <ReactDatePicker
        startDate={starDate?.[0]!}
        endDate={starDate?.[1]!}
        onChange={(dates) => setStartDate(dates)}
        monthsShown={2}
        placeholderText="Select Date in a Range"
        selectsRange
        inputProps={{
          clearable: true,
          onClear: () => setStartDate([null, null]),
        }}
      />
    </div>
  );
}
```

### Rizz UI Alert with Close Button (React)

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/0.8.7/feedback/alert

Demonstrates how to create a closable Alert component in React using the 'closable' prop and managing its visibility with the 'onClose' handler. This snippet shows a functional example of an informational alert that can be dismissed by the user.

```javascript
import React from "react";
import { Alert, Button } from "rizzui";

export default function App() {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = React.useState(true);
  return (
    <>
      <Button
        color="info"
        onClick={() => setIsOpen(true)}
        className="tracking-wider"
      >
        Info Alert
      </Button>
      {isOpen && (
        <Alert
          color="info"
          variant="flat"
          closable
          onClose={() => setIsOpen(false)}
        >
          <Text className="font-semibold">Alert with info</Text>
          <Text>
            Attention All! We are excited to announce the launch of our new product/service.
          </Text>
        </Alert>
      )}
    </>
  );
}
```

### RizzUI Password API Reference

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/0.8.7/Inputs/password

Comprehensive API documentation for the RizzUI Password component. Details all available props, their types, descriptions, default values, and related type definitions. Includes native HTML input attributes.

```APIDOC
Password Props:
  label: ReactNode | Set field label | __
  labelWeight: LabelWeight | Set label font weight | "medium"
  placeholder: string | Set input placeholder text | __
  variant: PasswordVariants | The variants of the component are: | "outline"
  size: PasswordSizes | The size of the component. "sm" is equivalent to the dense input styling. | "md"
  rounded: PasswordRoundeds | The rounded variants are: | "md"
  disabled: boolean | Whether the input is disabled or not | __
  clearable: boolean | Add clearable option | __
  hideVisibilityToggleIcon: boolean | Hides visibility toggle icon | __
  isPasswordVisible: boolean | Control password visibility from outside. | __
  onClear: PasswordOnclear | clear event | __
  prefix: ReactNode | The prefix is design for adding any icon or text on the Input field's start (it's a left icon for the `ltr` and right icon for the `rtl`) | __
  visibilityToggleIcon: ((visible: boolean) => ReactNode) | It is the password visibility toggle icon. | __
  helperText: ReactNode | Add helper text. It could be string or a React component | __
  error: string | Show error message using this prop | __
  labelClassName: string | Override default CSS style of label | __
  inputClassName: string | Override default CSS style of input | __
  prefixClassName: string | Override default CSS style of prefix | __
  visibilityToggleIconClassName: string | Override default CSS style of password show/hide toggle icon | __
  helperClassName: string | Override default CSS style of helperText | __
  errorClassName: string | Override default CSS style of error message | __
  className: string | Add custom classes to the root of the component | __
  ref: Ref<HTMLInputElement> |  | __
  ...: InputHTMLAttributes | native props like **value**, **onChange**, **onFocus**, **onBlur** ... | __

Password Variants Type:
  PasswordVariants = "outline" | "flat" | "text"

Label Weight Type:
  LabelWeight = "normal" | "medium" | "semibold" | "bold"

Password Sizes Type:
  PasswordSizes = "sm" | "md" | "lg" | "xl"

Password Rounded Type:
  PasswordRounded = "sm" | "md" | "lg" | "none" | "pill"

Password onClear Type:
  PasswordOnclear = (event) => void
```

--------------------------------

### RizzUI Password: External State Management

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/0.8.7/Inputs/password

Demonstrates how to manage the visibility state of the Password component externally using the `isPasswordVisible` prop. This example shows controlling the password's visibility with an external button, leveraging React's `useState` hook.

```javascript
import React from "";
import { Password, Flex, Button } from "rizzui";

export default function App() {
  const [showPassword, setShowPassword] = React.useState(false);
  return (
    <Flex
      align="end"
      justify="center"
    >
      <Password
        label="Visibility Toggle from outside"
        placeholder="Your password"
        hideVisibilityToggleIcon
        isPasswordVisible={showPassword}
        className="grow"
      />
      <Button onClick={() => setShowPassword(!showPassword)}>
        {showPassword ? "Hide" : "Show"}
      </Button>
    </Flex>
  );
}
```

### RizzUI Alert: Demonstrating Rounded Variants

Source: https://www.rizzui.com/docs/0.8.7/feedback/alert

This code snippet demonstrates how to customize the border radius of the RizzUI Alert component using the 'rounded' property. It includes examples for 'none', small ('sm'), large ('lg'), extra-large ('xl'), and the default roundedness, providing flexibility in styling the alert's corners.

```javascript
import { Alert, Text } from "rizzui";

export default function App() {
  return (
    <>

        color="success"

        </Text>
      </Alert>
      <Alert
        color="success"
        rounded="sm"
      >
        <Text className="font-semibold">Alert Rounded Small</Text>
        <Text>
          Attention All! We are excited to announce the launch of our new product/service.
        </Text>
      </Alert>
      <Alert color="success">
        <Text className="font-semibold">Alert Rounded Default</Text>
        <Text>
          Attention All! We are excited to announce the launch of our new product/service.
        </Text>
      </Alert>

        color="success"
        rounded="lg"

        </Text>
      </Alert>
      <Alert
        color="success"
        rounded="xl"
      >
        <Text className="font-semibold">Alert Rounded Extra Large</Text>

        </Text>

    </>
  );
```
